The spa on site was very nice and more affordable than other hotel spas -, the hotel also gave some coupons which was nice. You can access other places such as Dadonghai and Yalong Bay easily by taxi but there's not much around the hotel like restaurants. 

Overall: a good value for money in Sanya which can be very expensive.

posted:Posted January 27, 2024
msg:The hotel is located between Dadonghai and Yalong Bay, which is relatively remote. Taking a taxi to a closer place like Dadonghai costs more than 20 yuan. It takes about ten minutes to walk to the Xiangtu Village bus station. There are many buses. There are many residential buildings in the surrounding area, and there are also many people living there, mostly the elderly and children spending the winter. The supporting facilities are average and there is basically no larger catering.
The hotel is large in size, with two independent buildings, with its own yard and garden. Although the two buildings are not far away, there is a free shuttle bus. The facilities are a bit old, but they are worthy of the five-diamond rating. The comfortable twin room with mountain and sea view that I stayed in was in Building 2, which was relatively quiet, but all service facilities, such as the front desk, restaurant, spa, swimming pool, gym, etc., had to go to Building 1, which was also relatively lively. The room is large in size, has an independent balcony and a good view. It is fully equipped with refrigerator, ceiling fan, kitchen and other facilities. It is very comfortable to stay. The only dissatisfaction with the room is that the ventilation facility in the bathroom is just a hole, as shown in Figure 16. It has a weak sense of existence and is better than nothing.
The room service is very good, with a good attitude and attentiveness. Although I don't know the name, I would like to praise the waiter who has served us for a week.
The breakfast was okay, as shown in Figure 10. It was better than a four-star or four-diamond hotel, but it was just that. It was not outstanding, but it was quite comfortable. What I need to complain about is the buffet dinner. It has too few varieties, poor taste and is so expensive. It‚Äôs a bummer. I tried it once with high hopes but gave up decisively. This quality made me feel a loss for spending 68 yuan to eat it, and I still wanted 118 yuan.
All in all, if you want to spend a few days in a quiet place with beautiful scenery and expect high value for money, this hotel is a very good choice.
